Classifieds</a>\n                    </li>\n                    <li class=\"main-nav has-sub\">\n                        <a class=\"main-nav-item\" href=\n                          <a href=\n                                \"http://fashionwashington.com/?nid=menu_nav_partners-fashionwashington\">\n                                Fashion Washington</a>\n <header class=\"pg-header  pg-header--center\">\n\n    <div class=\"pg-kicker\">\n        <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/national/health-science/?utm_term=.6deb05e01e5c\">\n        \n            Health and Science\n        \n        </a>\n\n        \n    </div>\n\n    <h1 class=\"pg-h1\">\n        \n            How the House Republicans\u2019 proposed Obamacare replacement compares\n        \n    </h1>\n\n    <p class=\"pg-intro\">\n        \n            On Monday, House leaders released legislation to replace the Affordable Care Act. If it passes, here\u2019s what would change.\n        \n    </p>\n\n    <div class=\"pg-byline\">\n        <span class=\"pg-byline--author-wrap\">\n        By <a class=\"pg-byline--author\" href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/people/darla-cameron/?utm_term=.0d4db30ed1be\">Darla Cameron</a> and <a class=\"pg-byline--author\" href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/people/leslie-shapiro/\">Leslie Shapiro</a>\n        </span>\n\n        <div class=\"pg-pubDate\">\n            March 7, 2017\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <!-- SOCIAL TOOLS -->\n<div class=\n\"moat-trackable pb-f-theme-normal full pb-feature pb-layout-item pb-f-sharebars-top-share-bar\"\ndata-chain-name=\"no-name\" data-feature-id=\"sharebars/top-share-bar\"\ndata-feature-name=\"no-name\" id=\"f0dI3jX2uxHpTp\">\n    <style>\n    .hideText{position:absolute;left:-10000px}\n    </style>\n    \n    \n    <div class=\n        \"top-sharebar-wrapper vertical-sticky-top-sharebar\" data-pb-canonical-url=\n        \"https://www.washingtonpost.com/graphics/politics/how-aca-replacement-compares/\" data-pb-prevent-ajax=\"false\" data-postshare=\"facebook,twitter,google-plus,email,linkedin,tumblr,whatsapp,sms\" id=\"top-sharebar_2870\">\n        \n        <div class=\"social-tools-wrapper\">\n            <span class=\"social-tools-primary\"></span>\n            <div class=\"social-tools default-desktop\">\n                <span class=\"social-tools-primary\"><a onclick=\"var shareWindow=window.open('https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=http://wapo.st/2lBHgL0%3Ftid=ss_fb','share_facebook','width=658,height=354,scrollbars=no'); Please enable JavaScript for the best experience.</noscript>\n</header>\n\n\n            <article class=\"pg-article  col-lg-12 col-md-12 col-sm-12 col-xs-12 \" role=\"main\">\n\n            \n            \n                \n\n\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"subhead\">\n        \n        \n<div class=\"pg-skinny subhead\">\n\n    <h2 class=\"pg-h2 subhead\">Who would be covered</h2>\n    <p class=\"pg-bodyCopy centered\">\n\t    \n\t        Under two plans drafted by separate House committees, the government would no longer penalize Americans for failing to have health insurance.\n\t    \n\t</p>\n\n</div>\n\n\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  out \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3\"><i class='fa fa-times'></i> OUT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Enforcement of the <strong>individual mandate</strong> requiring coverage\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  in \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          <strong>30 percent surcharge</strong> on premiums that insurers would be able to impose on consumers who purchase a new plan after letting their previous coverage lapse \u2014 a strategy to encourage people to remain insured\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  out \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3\"><i class='fa fa-times'></i> OUT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          <strong>Employer mandate</strong> on larger companies to offer affordable coverage\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  hide \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"subhead\">\n        \n        \n<div class=\"pg-skinny subhead\">\n\n    <h2 class=\"pg-h2 subhead\">How they would pay for coverage</h2>\n    <p class=\"pg-bodyCopy centered\">\n\t    \n\t        The plans would do away with federal health insurance subsidies helping most people with ACA marketplace plans afford their monthly premiums and, in some cases, lowering out-of-pocket expenses.\n\t    \n\t</p>\n\n</div>\n\n\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  out \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3\"><i class='fa fa-times'></i> OUT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Tax credits, based on income, age, geography and other factors, that benefit <strong>lower and moderate-income people buying coverage through ACA marketplaces</strong>, would end in 2020\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  in \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Tax credits, based on income and age, for people <strong>buying on their own any health insurance</strong> sold in their state\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"text\">\n        \n        \n<div class=\"cutout pg-skinny centered\">\n\n\t<h3 class=\"pg-h3 subhead\">How the new tax credits would work</h3>\n\t<p class=\"pg-bodyCopy franklin textBlock\">\n\t    \n\t        The new legislation would break people into five age groups, each receiving a different amount in tax credits to purchase health insurance:\n<span><span>Age</span> <span><strong>Tax credit</strong></span></span>\n<span><span>20 \u2013 29:</span> <span><strong>$2,000</strong></span></span>\n<span><span>30 \u2013 39:</span> <span><strong>$2,500</strong></span></span>\n<span><span>40 \u2013 49:</span> <span><strong>$3,000</strong></span></span>\n<span><span>50 \u2013 59:</span> <span><strong>$3,500</strong></span></span>\n<span><span>60 and older:</span> <span><strong>$4,000</strong></span></span></p><p class=\"franklin pg-bodyCopy textBlock\">These credits begin to phase out for <strong>individuals making more than $75,000 and joint filers making over $150,000</strong>. Other restrictions include:</p><p class=\"franklin pg-bodyCopy textBlock\"><ul>\n<li>For each $1,000 in additional income above the limits, a person would be entitled to $100 less in credit.</li>\n<li>Credits would be limited to a maximum $14,000 per family.</li>\n<li>Credits could be used for any health plan allowed in a state, including ones providing only catastrophic coverage.</li>\n<li>Credits could not be used to buy health plans that cover abortion.</li>\n</ul>\n\t    \n\t</p>\n\n</div>\n\n\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  out \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3\"><i class='fa fa-times'></i> OUT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Insurers can <strong>charge older customers up to three times</strong> what they charge younger customers.\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  in \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Insurers would be able to <strong>charge older customers up to five times</strong> what they charge younger customers.\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  out \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3\"><i class='fa fa-times'></i> OUT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Individuals can contribute up to $3,400 and families up to $6,750 to pre-tax <strong>health savings accounts</strong>.\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  in \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Starting in 2018, individuals could contribute up to $6,550 and families could contribute up to $13,100 to pre-tax <strong>health savings accounts</strong>.\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  out \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3\"><i class='fa fa-times'></i> OUT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          <strong>Cost-sharing subsidies</strong>, which were provided to insurers to help their ACA customers cover deductibles and co-payments (ending in 2020)\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  hide \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell \">\n    \n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  in \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          States would receive $100 billion over 10 years through a new Patient and State Stability Fund for safety-net needs and possible <strong>\u201chigh-risk pools\u201d</strong> for consumers with expensive medical conditions.\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"subhead\">\n        \n        \n<div class=\"pg-skinny subhead\">\n\n    <h2 class=\"pg-h2 subhead\">Proposed changes to Medicaid</h2>\n    <p class=\"pg-bodyCopy centered\">\n\t    \n\t        Here\u2019s how the legislation would address Medicaid.\n\t    \n\t</p>\n\n</div>\n\n\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  out \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3\"><i class='fa fa-times'></i> OUT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Medicaid as an <strong>entitlement program</strong> with open-ended, matching federal funds for anyone who qualifies\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  in \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Medicaid would be funded by giving states a <strong>per-capita amount</strong> based on how much each state was spending for the fiscal year that ended in September.\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table-single-col\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper table-single-col cutout\"> \n  <h3 class=\"pg-h3 subhead\">How Medicaid expansion would be affected</h3>\n  <p class=\"pg-bodyCopy franklin pg-skinny\">Under Obamacare, <span class=\"medicaid-states\">31 states</span> broadened their Medicaid programs to cover people making up to 138 percent of poverty-level income.</p>\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6\"> \n    <p class=\"pg-bodyCopy franklin\">\n      \n          Under the GOP plans, the states would continue getting enhanced federal funding until 2020. After that, the government would keep paying 90 percent for beneficiaries already on the rolls as long as they remain eligible. Starting in 2020, new beneficiaries would be funded at a lower level.</p><p class=\"pg-bodyCopy franklin\">Also as of 2020, coverage of <strong>substance abuse and mental health services</strong> would no longer be required for this population.\n      \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  \n    <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 graphic graphic-svg\">\n      \n      \n<svg version=\"1.1\" id=\"Layer_1\" key elements of the plans</h2>\n    <p class=\"pg-bodyCopy centered\">\n\t    \n\t        The legislation would preserve some of the most popular features of the 2010 health-care law, while targeting Planned Parenthood.\n\t    \n\t</p>\n\n</div>\n\n\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf no-padding\"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell \">\n    \n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  kept \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i> KEPT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Insurers would still be banned from denying coverage based on <strong>preexisting conditions</strong>.\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf no-padding\"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell \">\n    \n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  kept \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i> KEPT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Dependents would still be able to stay on parents\u2019 insurance plans <strong>until age 26</strong>.\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf no-padding\"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell \">\n    \n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  kept \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i> KEPT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Caps on <strong>annual or lifetime coverage</strong> would still be banned.\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf no-padding\"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell \">\n    \n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  kept \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i> KEPT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Insurers would still have to cover certain categories of <strong>specified benefits</strong> first covered by the ACA.\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf no-padding\"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell \">\n    \n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  kept \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i> KEPT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Insurers would still be prohibited from discriminating on the basis of <strong>race, color, national origin, sex, age or disability</strong>. (For now, a federal judge has blocked enforcement of the provision as relates to gender identity and the termination of pregnancy.)\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"block\" data-block-type=\"table\">\n        \n        <div class=\"table-wrapper cf \"> \n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  out \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3\"><i class='fa fa-times'></i> OUT </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          <strong>Planned Parenthood</strong> is eligible for Medicaid reimbursements or federal family-planning grants (but federal money cannot fund abortions)\n          \n    </p>\n  </div>\n\n  <div class=\"col-md-6 col-sm-6 table-cell  in \">\n    <h3 class=\"pg-h3 in\"><i class='fa fa-check'></i>  IN </h3>\n    <p class=\"franklin\">\n          Planned Parenthood would face a <strong>one-year funding freeze</strong>\n    </p>\n  </div>\n  \n  \n</div>\n    </div>\n\n\n\n    <div class=\"pg-chart pg-border--bottom\">\n        <footer                 How the Republican plans to replace Obamacare could affect you\n                </a>\n            </h5>\n            <p>\n                Many analysts doubt whether the plans
